       <tr> 
        <td>
         <div id="mainContent"> 
          <p><strong>UCR Anthropology</strong> is committed to a socially engaged, critical anthropology that recognizes the importance of the sometimes contradictory unity of approaches to understanding the human condition in all its dimensions. It has a finely tuned sense of historical temporality that views change as normal as reproduction. It takes account of the existence and potential significance of the variability and diversity of human beings, as both social and natural beings in space, place, and time. It provides culture, ensembles of social relations, and the human body itself with sociohistorial contingency. It does not separate the historical development of human societies or the human species from the events, contradictions, and forces that shaped their development in time and space. It knows that human activity can effect significant change as witnessed by the diverse array of societies that existed in the past and continue to form the present. It acknowledges the complex interrelations of consciousness, communication, and the subjectivity of individuals in particular sets of social relations. It engages rather than shies away from the critical social, moral, and political issues of the day. It knows that people occasionally do make their own history, and that some trajectories of change potentially have better outcomes than others.</p> 
          <p>The faculty and students are committed to an integrated and integrating concept of the discipline. They view the traditional subfields—applied, archaeological, sociocultural, biological, and linguistic anthropology--as cross cut by foci that bring faculty and students together in ways that reinforce the unity of the discipline rather than its divisions. The foci articulate contemporary or emerging concerns among anthropologists and the wider public.</p> 
          <fieldset style="padding: 10px; border: 1px solid #CCC; background-color: #f5f5f5;">
           <legend style="font-size: 14px; font-weight: bold; color: #900;">Job Announcement</legend>

           </ul> 
          </fieldset>

           <p><a href="news_events/index.html">34th Annual James C. Young Colloquium: Rebellion as Transformation, March 14, 2014</a></p> 
          </fieldset>
          <br /> 
          <fieldset style="padding: 10px; border: 1px solid #CCC; background-color: #f5f5f5;"> 
           <legend style="font-size: 14px; font-weight: bold; color: #900;">In the News</legend> 
           <p>Professor Juliet McMullin and colleagues are awarded an NEH Humanities Initiatives grant to develop Health Humanities programing at UCR.</p> 
           <p>Professor Sally Ann Ness receives the Congress on Research in Dance 2013 Dixie Durr Award for Outstanding Service.</p> 
           <p>Professor Susan Ossman brings the <a href="http://movingmattersworkshops.com/" target="_blank"><em>Moving Matters Traveling Workshop</em></a> to Paris. Next stops: Amsterdam, Bogota and Berlin.</p> 
           <p>Professor Christina Schwenkel is quoted in an article in the Christian Science Monitor on <a href="http://www.csmonitor.com/layout/set/r14/USA/Society/2013/1110/Why-US-veterans-are-returning-to-Vietnam" target="_blank">US veterans returning to Vietnam</a>.</p> 
           <p>Professor Wendy Ashmore joins the UCR Academy of Distinguished Teachers 2013-2016</p>

      <div class="span12"> 
       <h1 class="page-header">Business Operations</h1> 
      </div> 
      <div class="span12"> 
       <ul class="nav nav-tabs sub-nav tab3"> 
        <li class="active"><a class="" href="index.html">Overview</a></li> 
        <li class=""><a class="" href="staff/index.html">Immediate Office Staff</a></li> 
        <li class=""><a class="" href="procedures-guidance/index.html">Procedures &amp; Guidance</a></li> 
       </ul> 
      </div> 
     </div> 
     <!-- Example row of columns --> 
     <div class="row-fluid"> 
      <div class="span4 hero-unit"> 
       <p>We oversee and develop policy for the university's business operations.</p> 
      </div> 
      <div class="span4">
       <p>The Executive Vice President of Business Operations serves as chief administrative officer for the University of California system, with responsibility over systemwide budget, facility construction and maintenance, real estate management, human resource administration and information technology support. This office also oversees the budget and administration of the Office of the President.</p>
      </div> 
      <div class="span4"> 
       <div class="row-fluid dotted-bottom"> 
        <div class="span4 dept-head"> 
         <img alt="Nathan Brostrom" src="_files/shot_11_nbrostrom_010.jpg" />
        </div> 
        <div class="span8"> 
         <p class="blue"> <a href="staff/bios/nathan-brostrom.html">Nathan Brostrom</a> </p> 
         <p>Executive Vice President</p> 
        </div> 
       </div> 
       <div class="row-fluid"> 
        <div class="span6"> 
         <a class="icon staff" href="staff/index.html">Staff Directory</a>
        </div> 
        <div class="span6"> 
         <a class="icon org" href="_files/busops_orgchart.pdf">Org Chart</a>
        </div> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
     </div> 
     <div class="row-fluid blustripe dept-unit"> 
      <h2 class="nobtm">DEPARTMENTS</h2> 
      <div class="row-fluid col5"> 
       <div class="span4"> 
        <h3 class="blue"> <a href="/budget-capital-resources/index.html">Budget &amp; Capital Resources</a> </h3> 
        <p>Supports and provides recommendations to the President and the campuses in the effective utilization, allocation and management of systemwide resources.</p> 
        <dl class="top-dest"> 
         <dt>
          Top Destinations
         </dt> 
         <dd>

         </dd>

         </dd>

          <a href="/real-estate-services/index.html">Real Estate Services</a> 
         </dd>

         </dd> 
         <dd> 
          <a href="/operating-budget/index.html">Operating Budget</a> 
         </dd> 
        </dl> 
       </div> 
       <div class="span4"> 
        <h3 class="blue"> <a href="/human-resources/index.html">Human Resources</a> </h3> 
        <p>Manages systemwide human resources and benefits, employee and labor relations, compensation and performance, workforce development and compliance.</p> 
        <dl class="top-dest"> 
         <dt>
          Top Destinations
         </dt> 
         <dd> 
          <a href="/human-resources/staff/index.html">Systemwide Human Resources staff</a> 
         </dd>

         </dd>

         </dd> 
         <dd>

         </dd> 
         <dd> 
          <a href="http://atyourservice.ucop.edu">At Your Service</a> 
         </dd> 
         <dd> 
          <a href="/local-human-resources/index.html">UCOP local human resources</a> 
         </dd> 
        </dl> 
       </div> 
       <div class="span4"> 
        <h3 class="blue"> <a href="/information-technology-services/index.html">Information Technology Services</a> </h3> 
        <p>Provides information technology (IT) services for UC campuses and the Office of the President, from corporate data systems to telecommunications to computer networks.</p> 
        <dl class="top-dest"> 
         <dt>
          Top Destinations
         </dt> 
         <dd> 
          <a href="/information-technology-services/services/index.html">Support services</a> 
         </dd> 
         <dd> 
          <a href="/information-technology-services/policies/index.html">Policies &amp; guidelines</a> 
         </dd> 
         <dd> 
          <a href="/information-technology-services/services/announcement/index.html">Announcements</a> 
         </dd> 
         <dd> 
          <a href="/information-technology-services/services/user-agreement/index.html">User agreement</a>

       </div>

     <div class="row-fluid blustripe dept-unit"> 
      <h2 class="nobtm">IMMEDIATE OFFICE UNITS</h2> 
      <div class="row-fluid col5"> 
       <div class="span3"> 
        <h3 class="blue"> <a href="/building-administrative-services/index.html">Building &amp; Administrative Service Center (BASC)</a> </h3> 
        <p>Provides a clean, safe and secure working environment and efficient administrative support for OP.</p> 
        <dl class="top-dest"> 
         <dt>
          Top Destinations
         </dt> 
         <dd> 
          <a href="/building-administrative-services/employee-systems/index.html">Employee systems</a> 
         </dd> 
         <dd> 
          <a href="/building-administrative-services/services/index.html">All BASC services</a> 
         </dd> 
        </dl> 
       </div> 
       <div class="span3"> 
        <h3 class="blue"> <a href="/center-operations-excellence/index.html">Center for Operations Excellence (COPE)</a> </h3> 
        <p>Helps UCOP departments develop organizational change strategies to meet current and future business demands.</p> 
        <dl class="top-dest"> 
         <dt>
          Top Destinations
         </dt> 
         <dd> 
          <a href="/center-operations-excellence/services/index.html">COPE services</a> 
         </dd> 
         <dd> 
          <a href="/center-operations-excellence/resources/index.html">Change management resources</a> 
         </dd> 
        </dl> 
       </div> 
       <div class="span3"> 
        <h3 class="blue"> <a href="/strategic-resources-group/index.html">Strategic Resources Group</a> </h3> 
        <p>Coordinates UCOP project management, business analysis and change management resources.</p> 
        <dl class="top-dest"> 
         <dt>
          Top Destinations
         </dt> 
         <dd> 
          <a href="/strategic-resources-group/services/index.html">SRG services</a> 
         </dd> 
         <dd> 
          <a href="/strategic-resources-group/projects/index.html">New and completed projects </a> 
         </dd> 
         <dd> 
          <a href="/strategic-resources-group/resources/index.html">Project management resources</a> 
         </dd> 
        </dl> 
       </div> 
       <div class="span3"> 
        <h3 class="blue"> <a href="/ucop-budget/index.html">UCOP Budget Office</a> </h3> 
        <p>Develops, monitors and manages the UCOP budget program, systematically aligning resources with strategic needs and goals.</p> 
        <dl class="top-dest"> 
         <dt>
          Top Destinations
         </dt> 
         <dd> 
          <a href="/ucop-budget/forms-procedures/index.html">Forms and procedures</a> 
         </dd> 
         <dd> 
          <a href="/ucop-budget/budget-development/index.html">Budget development tools</a> 
         </dd> 
        </dl> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
     </div>

        // Google WaterMark Script
        $(function () {
            $("#txtGoogleSearch").each(function () {
                ToggleHint($(this)); // add class on page load to elements with "hintable" class
            });

            $("#txtGoogleSearch").focus(function () {
                $(this).removeClass("GoogleWatermark"); // handle all focus hints
            });

            $("#txtGoogleSearch").blur(function () {
                ToggleHint(this); // handle all blur hints
            });
        });

        function ToggleHint(obj) {
            if ($(obj).val() == '') { $(obj).addClass("GoogleWatermark"); };
        }

     <img src="/Images/registering-for-classes.png" alt="" class="page-lead" /> 
     <script src="/Scripts/VerticalSlider.js"></script> 
     <div class="span-18"> 
      <h3>When to Register</h3> 
     </div> 
     <div class="span-9"> 
      <p>Start registering for classes at your initial enrollment appointment time*. See the <a href="../academic-calendar/Default.aspx">academic calendar</a> to find out when you can see your appointment time in <a href="http://growl.ucr.edu" target="_blank">Growl.</a> </p> 
      <p>You may register during <strong>initial </strong>and <strong>makeup</strong> enrollment. During <strong>initial </strong>enrollment, undergraduate students may register for a maximum of 17 units. During <strong>makeup</strong> enrollment, the maximum for undergraduate students is increased according to the college in which you belong. Remember, <a href="/registrar/registering-for-classes/waitlist-information.aspx">waitlist units</a> count toward your max. See the <a href="../academic-calendar/Default.aspx">academic calendar</a> for all registration phases. </p> 
      <p><a href="http://growl.ucr.edu" target="_blank">Growl</a> is normally available from 8 a.m. to 11:30 p.m., Monday through Friday. The system availability may vary due to system maintenance and nightly processing; therefore, we recommend you try to complete your enrollment activity before 5 p.m. Saturday and Sunday hours also vary depending on system maintenance. </p> 
      <p>&nbsp;</p> 
      <h3>How to Register</h3> 
     </div> 
     <div class="span-9 last"> 
      <div class="sidebar"> 
       <span class="warning">IMPORTANT:</span> 
       <img style="float: right;" src="../../Images/paperpushpin.png" alt="" /> 
       <ul class="orange-bullets"> 
        <li>You may add/drop/change/wait-list for classes in <a href="http://growl.ucr.edu" target="_blank">Growl</a> through week two of instruction. After that, it's an <a href="enrollment-adjustments.aspx">enrollment adjustment.</a> </li> 
        <li>Class codes: (M) Mon, (T) Tues, (W) Weds, (R) Thurs, (F) Fri , (S) Sat. </li> 
        <li>If a class has a <a href="course-requisites.aspx">co-requisite</a>, enroll in it when you enroll in the lecture.</li> 
        <li>You will be disconnected after 10 minutes of inactivity. </li> 
        <li>Plan ahead for alternate courses.</li> 
        <li>If you are physically unable to use Growl, contact <a href="http://specialservices.ucr.edu/contact/Pages/default.aspx" target="_blank">Student Special Services</a>.</li> 
        <li>Protect your PERMPIN and log out before leaving your computer! </li> 
       </ul> 
      </div> 
     </div> 
     <div class="wizard-wrapper" style="margin-top: 220px"> 
      <div class="wizard-content border1px" style="margin-top: 20px; padding-top: 20px; width: 378px; min-height: 335px; float: right; margin-right: 20px"> 
       <div id="tab1" class="verticalslider_contents verticalSliderContentPadleft20"> 
        <h3>Log In To Growl</h3> 
        <p> Log in to <a href="http://growl.ucr.edu" target="_blank">Growl</a> with your student ID number, permanent personal identification number (PERMPIN) and birth date. You can also log in to <a href="http://rweb.ucr.edu/" target="_blank">R’Web</a> if you want to log in to R’Mail and Growl at the same time.<br /> <br /> <strong>Forget your PERMPIN?</strong> Call us at 951-827-7284 or come to the Highlander One Stop Shop (HOSS) on the first floor of the Student Services Building. Bring a valid photo ID.<br /> <br /> <strong>Forget your student ID number?</strong> Log in to <a href="http://growl.ucr.edu" target="_blank">Growl</a> with your SSN and PERMPIN and you will be able to retrieve it.<br /> <br /> </p> 
       </div> 
       <div id="tab2" class="verticalslider_contents verticalSliderContentPadleft20"> 
        <h3>Resolve Your Holds</h3> 
        <p> If you have outstanding <a href="/registrar/registering-for-classes/holds.aspx">holds</a>, a box will appear letting you know right away. The department initiating the hold must lift it before you can register for classes. You can also go to “Holds” on the left side of the <a href="http://growl.ucr.edu" target="_blank">Growl</a> screen to see all that apply to you.<br /> <br /> </p> 
       </div> 
       <div id="tab3" class="verticalslider_contents verticalSliderContentPadleft20"> 
        <h3>Select &quot;Advising/Enrollment&quot;</h3> 
        <p> Select &quot;Advising/Enrollment.&quot; Choose the appropriate quarter and take note of any registration information that appears including <a href="/registrar/registering-for-classes/advising-requirements.aspx">advising requirements</a>. <br /> <br /> </p> 
       </div> 
       <div id="tab4" class="verticalslider_contents verticalSliderContentPadleft20"> 
        <h3>Add, Drop, Change or Wait-List for Classes</h3> 
        <h3 class="shadowOrigFont"> <br /> Add a Class</h3> 
        <strong>1.</strong> Enter the class number in one &quot;Add&quot; section of the action menu. If a 
        <a href="/registrar/registering-for-classes/course-requisites.aspx">co-requisite</a> discussion or lab section is required, enter that number on another &quot;Add&quot; line. If there is room in the class, and you meet all requirements, the course status will read &quot;Enrolled,” and you will be registered in it.
        <br /> 
        <strong>2.</strong> If the class has variable units, you will see a box showing the minimum number available. Enter the appropriate number of units.
        <br /> 
        <strong>3.</strong> Click &quot;OK&quot; now, or after you have completed all of your enrollment activity.
        <br /> 
        <br /> 
        <h3 class="shadowOrigFont">Drop a Class</h3> 
        <p> Select &quot;Drop&quot; from the action menu. Remember to also drop any connected lab or discussion sections. Click &quot;OK.&quot; Course status should now read &quot;Dropped.&quot; You are allowed to drop classes through the second week of instruction. After that, it’s called “withdrawing” from a class and requires extra steps. See <a href="enrollment-adjustments.aspx">Enrollment Adjustments</a> for details.<br /> </p> 
        <h3 class="shadowOrigFont">Change a Discussion or Lab Section</h3> 
        <p>Select &quot;Change Sec&quot; from the action menu. Click &quot;OK.&quot; You will be presented with a list of open sections. You may choose a section from that list or keep the section in which you are already enrolled. Click “OK” again after you have made your choice.</p> 
        <h3 class="shadowOrigFont">Add or Remove Yourself From a Waitlist</h3> Please see 
        <a href="waitlist-information.aspx">Waitlist Information.</a>
        <br /> 
        <br /> 
       </div> 
       <div id="tab5" class="verticalslider_contents verticalSliderContentPadleft20"> 
        <h3>Review Your Classes and Exit Securely</h3> 
        <p> Check &quot;Classes&quot; before exiting to make sure your schedule looks correct. If everything looks all right, exit Growl, clear your cache and quit your Web browser. </p> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <div class="wizard-sidebar marginBtmMenu10Li borderLtTpBt1px" style="margin-top: 20px; width: 269px; float: left;"> 
       <ul class="verticalslider_tabs menuLiBlockText"> 
        <li id="loginGrowl" name="tab1" class="selected"><span>Step&nbsp;1 :</span>Log In To Growl</li> 
        <li id="holds" name="tab2"><span>Step 2 :</span>Resolve Your Holds</li> 
        <li id="selectAdvising" name="tab3"><span>Step 3 :</span>Select &quot;Advising/Enrollment&quot;</li> 
        <li id="addDropChange" name="tab4"><span>Step 4 :</span>Add, Drop, Change or Wait-list for Classes</li> 
        <li id="reviewClasses" style="margin-bottom:0px;" name="tab5"><span>Step 5 :</span>Review Your Classes and Exit Securely
         <div style="margin-top: -19px;"></div> </li> 
       </ul> 
      </div> 
      <div style="clear: both"></div> 
      <div class="span-18" last=""> 
       <br /> 
       <br /> 
       <h3>A Note on Attendance</h3> 
       <p>If you do not attend class during the first and second weeks of instruction, you may be dropped from the course or receive an “F” or “NC.” To avoid this, drop the class using <a href="http://growl.ucr.edu" target="_blank">Growl</a> (if it’s before week three) or file an <a href="enrollment-adjustments.aspx">enrollment adjustment</a><a href="enrollment-adjustments.aspx"> form</a> (if it’s week three or after). Refer to individual course listings for specific information about drops for nonattendance. Class listings in the <a href="../schedule-of-classes/Classes.aspx">class schedule</a> identify courses with mandatory attendance policies. Contact the academic department involved for more information about policies affecting specific courses. </p> 
       <p>* <em>Earned units determine appointment times (students with more register first). Pending transfer units do not count as earned units until official transcripts are processed. Priority registration is reserved for: Regents and Chancellor's Scholars, students with disabilities, foster youth, graduate students, student athletes/team managers, University Honors students and veterans/military. </em></p> 
      </div> 
     </div> 
    </div>

  <div class="pagewrapper"> 
   <h3 class="accessibility">Footer</h3> 
   <div id="colophon">
     The University of California, Riverside (
    <a href="http://www.ucr.edu/">www.ucr.edu</a>) is a doctoral research university, a living laboratory for groundbreaking exploration of issues critical to Inland Southern California, the state and communities around the world. Reflecting California's diverse culture, UCR's enrollment has exceeded 21,000 students. The campus opened a medical school in 2013 and has reached the heart of the Coachella Valley by way of the UCR Palm Desert Center. The campus has an annual statewide economic impact of more than $1 billion. A broadcast studio with fiber cable to the AT&amp;T Hollywood hub is available for live or taped interviews. UCR also has ISDN for radio interviews. To learn more, call (951) UCR-NEWS. 
   </div>
